### Historical Resolved Issues[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#historical-resolved-issues "Copy heading link")

#### React Hooks Crisis (April 2026)[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#react-hooks-crisis-april-2026 "Copy heading link")

- **Issue**: "Rendered more hooks than during the previous render" error
- **Cause**: Conditional rendering of components containing hooks (Desktop vs Mobile)
- **Fix**: Component Separation Pattern - all device-specific logic in separate leaf components
- **Documentation**: PORT_DOCUMENTATION.md, DEVELOPER_GUIDE.md

#### PowerShell vs Node Conflict[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#powershell-vs-node-conflict "Copy heading link")

- **Issue**: Using `&&` or `||` in PowerShell scripts causes syntax errors
- **Fix**: Always use `cmd /c` for complex chaining in .bat files
- **Documentation**: SLAMZ_HANDOFF.md

#### Cinematic Pure Gating[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#cinematic-pure-gating "Copy heading link")

- **Issue**: POGs discovered multiple times, prize UI during bullet-time
- **Fix**: State sequestration - Showcase locked to `gameState === 'ROUND_JACKPOT'`
- **Documentation**: SLAMZ_HANDOFF.md

#### POG Falling Through Floor[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#pog-falling-through-floor "Copy heading link")

- **Issue**: POGs tunneling through floor at high velocities
- **Fix**: Replaced Trimesh floor collider with CylinderCollider primitive
- **Documentation**: AGENT_CHANGES.md, SLAMZ_HANDOFF.md

#### Showcase.tsx Corruption[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#showcasetsx-corruption "Copy heading link")

## PERFORMANCE CONSIDERATIONS[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#performance-considerations "Copy heading link")

### Performance Monitoring[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#performance-monitoring "Copy heading link")

**Components**:

- `PerformanceMonitor.tsx`: FPS counter and metrics
- `AdaptiveQuality.tsx`: Dynamic quality adjustment

### Device Performance Detection[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#device-performance-detection "Copy heading link")

**Location**: `src/utils/devicePerformance.ts`

- **ENABLE_ANTIALIAS**: Based on device capability
- **CANVAS_DPR**: Device pixel ratio clamping

### Mobile Performance[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#mobile-performance "Copy heading link")

**Location**: `src/utils/mobilePerformance.ts`

- FPS tracking
- Memory monitoring
- Quality scaling

### Optimization Strategies[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#optimization-strategies "Copy heading link")

1. **Memoization**: PhysicsInnerScene memoized for GPU buffer stability
2. **Object Pooling**: Reusable THREE objects in useFrame (no `new` in loops)
3. **Render Throttling**: StartScreen throttles to once per 3 seconds after intro
4. **Fixed Timestep**: Physics uses fixed 1/60 timestep for stability
5. **CCD**: Continuous collision detection prevents tunneling
6. **Component Separation**: Prevents unnecessary re-renders

### Known Performance Bottlenecks[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=9127e542-5286-4b93-8a67-2bbaf49434b1&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#known-performance-bottlenecks "Copy heading link")

- **Texture Generation**: Synchronous during init (acceptable for load time)
- **Physics Solver**: 12 iterations + 4 PGS iterations (tunable)
- **Post-Processing**: CRT effects can be heavy on low-end devices

#### Legal Implications[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#legal-implications "Copy heading link")

**Trademark Issues**:

- Mortal Kombat is a trademark of Warner Bros. Interactive Entertainment
- Teenage Mutant Ninja Turtles is a trademark of Viacom/Nickelodeon
- Street Fighter is a trademark of Capcom

**Copyright Issues**:

- Character likenesses are copyrighted
- Using these without permission is copyright infringement
- Even for a jam entry, this is legally risky

**Vibe Jam Context**:

- Jam entries often have more leniency
- But commercial use would definitely require licenses
- Even non-commercial use can face C&D letters

#### Recommendation[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#recommendation "Copy heading link")

- **Priority**: HIGH
- **Action**:
    1. Replace with original characters/themes before commercial use
    2. For jam submission: acknowledge IP in credits
    3. Consider fair use arguments (but they're weak)
    4. Best approach: Create original IP

---

### Missing LICENSE File[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#missing-license-file "Copy heading link")

**Status**: No LICENSE file exists  
**Impact**: Default copyright applies  
**Risk**: Ambiguous usage rights

#### What This Means[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#what-this-means "Copy heading link")

- Without a LICENSE file, the project has default copyright
- Default = "all rights reserved"
- No one can legally use, modify, or distribute the code
- Even for open-source, you need a license

#### Recommendation[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#recommendation-1 "Copy heading link")

- **Priority**: HIGH
- **Action**: Add a LICENSE file
- **Options**:
    - MIT License (permissive, popular)
    - Apache 2.0 (patent protection)
    - GPL (copyleft, restrictive)
- **Recommended**: MIT for maximum flexibility

---

## 🚨 CRITICAL: Deployment URL Hardcoded[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#-critical-deployment-url-hardcoded "Copy heading link")

### Issue in index.html[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#issue-in-indexhtml "Copy heading link")

**Lines 10-18**:

```html
<meta property="og:url" content="https://slamz-pro-tour.vercel.app/" />
<meta property="twitter:url" content="https://slamz-pro-tour.vercel.app/" />
```

#### Problem[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#problem "Copy heading link")

- URL is hardcoded to Vercel
- If deploying elsewhere, social sharing will break
- Open Graph and Twitter cards will point to wrong URL

#### Recommendation[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#recommendation-2 "Copy heading link")

- **Priority**: MEDIUM
- **Action**:
    1. Make URL configurable via environment variable
    2. Or update during build process
    3. Or use relative URLs where possible

## ⚠️ IMPORTANT: Accessibility Issues[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#-important-accessibility-issues "Copy heading link")

### Viewport Locking[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#viewport-locking "Copy heading link")

**Line 6 in index.html**:

```html
<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, user-scalable=no, viewport-fit=cover" />
```

#### Problem[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#problem-1 "Copy heading link")

- `user-scalable=no` prevents zooming
- Violates WCAG accessibility guidelines
- Bad for users with vision impairments
- Some browsers ignore this anyway

#### Recommendation[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#recommendation-3 "Copy heading link")

- **Priority**: MEDIUM
- **Action**: Remove `user-scalable=no` and `maximum-scale=1.0`
- **Reason**: Accessibility compliance
- **Impact**: Users can zoom if needed

### Missing Accessibility Features[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#missing-accessibility-features "Copy heading link")

#### What's Missing[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#whats-missing "Copy heading link")

- No ARIA labels
- No keyboard navigation for game controls
- No screen reader support
- No focus management
- No high contrast mode

#### Current State[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#current-state "Copy heading link")

- **Accessibility**: Minimal
- **Testing**: None
- **Compliance**: Not WCAG compliant

#### Recommendation[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#recommendation-4 "Copy heading link")

- **Priority**: LOW (game is visual-heavy)
- **Action**: Consider basic accessibility if targeting wider audience
- **Note**: Full 3D games are inherently difficult to make accessible

## ℹ️ LOW: AI-Generated Assets[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#-low-ai-generated-assets "Copy heading link")

### og_preview.png C2PA Metadata[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#ogpreviewpng-c2pa-metadata "Copy heading link")

**Finding**: The og_preview.png has C2PA metadata indicating it was generated by Google Generative AI

#### What This Means[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#what-this-means-1 "Copy heading link")

- Image is AI-generated
- Has invisible watermark (SynthID)
- Metadata includes generation timestamp
- Metadata includes Google C2PA certificates

#### Implications[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#implications "Copy heading link")

- **Copyright**: AI-generated content copyright is unclear
- **Watermark**: SynthID watermark is invisible but detectable
- **Attribution**: Google metadata embedded in file

#### Recommendation[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#recommendation-9 "Copy heading link")

- **Priority**: LOW
- **Action**:
    1. Be aware of AI generation
    2. Consider if this matters for your use case
    3. Watermark doesn't affect visual appearance

## CONCLUSION[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#conclusion "Copy heading link")

You now have **5 comprehensive documents** covering literally everything about the SLAMZ/POGS project:

1. **Complete Technical Breakdown** - Codebase architecture, systems, physics, UI, audio, assets, cinematic engine, known issues, errors/fixes, development workflow, performance, debug tools, deployment, roadmap
    
2. **Git Repository Complete Breakdown** - Commits, history, patterns, repository health, development patterns, author statistics, timeline, file changes, LFS assets
    
3. **Team Survival Guide** - Critical warnings, environment setup, codebase gotchas, build traps, performance landmines, debugging nightmares, asset pipeline, state management, UI fragility, physics quirks, cinematic complexity, browser compatibility, testing, deployment, documentation corruptions, agent rules, emergency procedures
    
4. **Missing Infrastructure & Operational Risks** - No CI/CD, no testing, no code style enforcement, no security scanning, no backup strategy, no rollback procedure, no monitoring, launcher scripts, infrastructure roadmap
    
5. **Final Considerations & Legal/IP Notes** - Intellectual property issues (copyrighted characters), missing LICENSE file, hardcoded deployment URL, accessibility issues, missing community files, font licensing, AI-generated assets
    

### The Most Critical Issue[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#the-most-critical-issue "Copy heading link")

**The copyrighted character assets in the POG textures are a significant legal risk.** For a jam entry, it might be tolerated. For any commercial use or wider distribution, you must replace them with original IP or obtain proper licenses.

### Everything Else[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=8805d9b6-d843-4e2c-95f3-3eec2046903a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#everything-else "Copy heading link")

### Commit Message Patterns[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#commit-message-patterns "Copy heading link")

#### Conventional Commits Used[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#conventional-commits-used "Copy heading link")

- `feat:` - New features
- `fix:` - Bug fixes
- `chore:` - Maintenance tasks
- `perf(P0):` - Performance optimizations (priority tagged)
- `docs:` - Documentation updates

- **Descriptive**: Clear, detailed messages
- **Context**: Includes scope and impact

- **Length**: Appropriate detail level

### Strengths[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#strengths "Copy heading link")

1. **Linear History**: Clean, easy to follow
2. **Descriptive Commits**: Clear commit messages
3. **LFS Integration**: Proper large file management
4. **No Merge Conflicts**: Smooth development
5. **Single Branch**: Simplified workflow
6. **Active Development**: Recent commits (April 2026)

### Areas for Improvement[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#areas-for-improvement "Copy heading link")

1. **No Tags**: Missing release tags for versioning
2. **No Feature Branches**: All work on main (risky for larger projects)
3. **No Pull Requests**: Direct commits reduce review opportunities
4. **No CI/CD**: No automated testing/deployment visible
5. **Large Commits**: Some commits are very large (e.g., 09ab53c)

### Risks[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#risks "Copy heading link")

1. **Single Branch**: No isolation for experimental features
2. **Direct Commits**: No code review process
3. **No Rollback Strategy**: No tags for easy rollback
4. **Large Binary Files**: LFS dependency for 3D assets

### Commit Patterns[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#commit-patterns "Copy heading link")

#### Frequency[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#frequency "Copy heading link")

- **Peak**: 9 commits in one day (April 16)
- **Average**: 4.17 commits/day
- **Burst Development**: Intensive sprints

#### Commit Size[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#commit-size "Copy heading link")

- **Small**: Typical (1-10 files, <100 lines)
- **Medium**: Frequent (10-30 files, 100-1000 lines)
- **Large**: Occasional (30+ files, 1000+ lines)
- **Massive**: Rare (50+ files, 5000+ lines)

#### Time Distribution[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#time-distribution "Copy heading link")

- **Morning Commits**: Frequent
- **Afternoon Commits**: Frequent
- **Evening Commits**: Occasional
- **Late Night**: Some (April 15-16)

### Development Workflow[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#development-workflow "Copy heading link")

#### Typical Pattern[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#typical-pattern "Copy heading link")

1. Feature implementation (multiple small commits)
2. Bug fixes (immediate commits)
3. Performance optimization (focused commits)
4. Cleanup (batched commits)
5. Documentation (final commits)

#### Iteration Style[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=b4c9499d-adde-42cd-8d86-63dbf2e0ab4a&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#iteration-style "Copy heading link")

- **Rapid Prototyping**: Fast iteration
- **Immediate Fixes**: Bugs addressed quickly
- **Batch Refactoring**: Cleanup in batches
- **Feature Completion**: Commits mark milestones

## WHAT'S MISSING (AND WHY IT MATTERS)[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#whats-missing-and-why-it-matters "Copy heading link")

### 🚨 CRITICAL: No CI/CD Pipeline[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#-critical-no-cicd-pipeline "Copy heading link")

**Status**: Completely absent  
**Impact**: All deployments are manual  
**Risk**: Human error, inconsistent deployments, no rollback capability

#### What This Means[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#what-this-means "Copy heading link")

- No GitHub Actions
- No GitLab CI
- No CircleCI
- No automated testing
- No automated builds
- No automated deployments

#### Operational Impact[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#operational-impact "Copy heading link")

- **Deployment**: Manual `npm run build` + manual file upload
- **Testing**: Manual only (no automated test runs)
- **Quality**: No automated linting/type-checking in pipeline
- **Rollback**: Manual git revert (no tagged releases)
- **Monitoring**: No deployment success/failure tracking

#### Recommendation[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#recommendation "Copy heading link")

- **Priority**: HIGH
- **Action**: Add GitHub Actions for:
    - Automated builds on push
    - TypeScript checking
    - Linting (if ESLint added)
    - Deployment to preview environment
    - Tagged release automation

### 🚨 CRITICAL: No Testing Infrastructure[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#-critical-no-testing-infrastructure "Copy heading link")

**Status**: Completely absent  
**Impact**: No automated regression testing  
**Risk**: Bugs in production, no safety net

#### What's Missing[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#whats-missing "Copy heading link")

- No test framework (Jest, Vitest, etc.)
- No test files
- No test coverage reports
- No E2E testing (Playwright, Cypress)
- No visual regression testing

#### Current State[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#current-state "Copy heading link")

- **Testing**: Manual only
- **Regression**: Relies on developer memory
- **Coverage**: 0% automated
- **Confidence**: Low

#### Recommendation[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#recommendation-1 "Copy heading link")

- **Priority**: HIGH
- **Action**: Add Vitest for:
    - Critical path testing (physics settle detection)
    - State machine transitions
    - Component rendering
    - Utility functions

### 🚨 CRITICAL: No Environment Variables[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#-critical-no-environment-variables "Copy heading link")

**Status**: Not applicable (actually good)  
**Impact**: None  
**Risk**: None

#### What This Means[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#what-this-means-1 "Copy heading link")

- No `.env` files
- No `.env.example`
- No secret management needed
- All configuration in code or localStorage

#### Why This is OK[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#why-this-is-ok "Copy heading link")

- **Client-side only**: No backend
- **No secrets**: No API keys, database credentials
- **Simple**: Fewer moving parts
- **Portable**: Easy to set up anywhere

#### Note[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#note "Copy heading link")

- If adding backend later, will need environment variables
- Currently: Keep as-is (simplicity is good)

### ⚠️ IMPORTANT: No Node Version Lock[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#-important-no-node-version-lock "Copy heading link")

**Status**: Missing `.nvmrc` or `.node-version`  
**Impact**: Version drift possible  
**Risk**: "Works on my machine" syndrome

#### What's Missing[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#whats-missing-1 "Copy heading link")

- No `.nvmrc` file
- No `.node-version` file
- No `.tool-versions` file
- No Node version specified in package.json engines

#### Current State[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#current-state-1 "Copy heading link")

- **Node Version**: Unknown (not specified)
- **Team Risk**: Different developers using different Node versions
- **CI Risk**: CI might use different Node version than local

#### Recommendation[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#recommendation-2 "Copy heading link")

- **Priority**: MEDIUM
- **Action**: Add `.nvmrc` with Node 18 LTS:
    
    ```bash
    echo "18" > .nvmrc
    ```
    
- **Benefit**: Ensures consistent Node version across team

## LAUNCHER SCRIPTS (Windows-Specific)[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#launcher-scripts-windows-specific "Copy heading link")

### What Exists[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#what-exists "Copy heading link")

1. **LAUNCH_GAME.bat** - Simple launcher
    
    - Checks if server running
    - Starts if not
    - Opens browser
    - Port 4173
2. **Silent_Launch_Slamz.vbs** - Silent wrapper
    
    - Runs launcher without console window
    - For desktop icon use
3. **Purge_Ghosts.bat** - Process killer
    
    - Kills all node.exe processes
    - Kills processes on port 4173
    - Useful when dev server gets stuck
4. **INSTALL_DESKTOP_ICON.bat** - Icon installer
    
    - Creates desktop shortcut
    - Uses slamz_icon.png
    - Points to Slamz_Desktop_Launcher.bat
5. **Slamz_Desktop_Launcher.bat** - Full launcher
    
    - Kills stale processes
    - Starts server in background
    - Waits for server ready
    - Opens browser

### Platform Limitation[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#platform-limitation "Copy heading link")

**Critical**: All launchers are Windows-only (.bat/.vbs)

- **macOS**: No equivalent scripts
- **Linux**: No equivalent scripts
- **Impact**: Non-Windows developers must use `npm run dev` manually

### Recommendation[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#recommendation-10 "Copy heading link")

- **Priority**: LOW (if team is Windows-only)
- **Action**: If supporting macOS/Linux, add shell scripts
- **Benefit**: Cross-platform development support

## RECOMMENDED INFRASTRUCTURE ROADMAP[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#recommended-infrastructure-roadmap "Copy heading link")

### Phase 1: Critical (Week 1)[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#phase-1-critical-week-1 "Copy heading link")

1. Add `.nvmrc` for Node version lock
2. Add basic ESLint configuration
3. Add git tags for current release
4. Document rollback procedure

### Phase 2: Important (Week 2-3)[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#phase-2-important-week-2-3 "Copy heading link")

1. Add GitHub Actions for CI
2. Add Vitest for critical path testing
3. Add Dependabot for security
4. Add pre-commit hooks (husky + lint-staged)

### Phase 3: Nice-to-Have (Month 1)[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#phase-3-nice-to-have-month-1 "Copy heading link")

1. Add Sentry for error tracking
2. Add bundle size monitoring
3. Add performance monitoring
4. Add cross-platform launcher scripts

### Phase 4: Advanced (Month 2+)[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#phase-4-advanced-month-2 "Copy heading link")

1. Add E2E testing (Playwright)
2. Add visual regression testing
3. Add automated deployment
4. Add canary releases

## SUMMARY[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#summary "Copy heading link")

### What You Have (Good)[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#what-you-have-good "Copy heading link")

- Clean, simple architecture
- No environment variable complexity
- Working launcher scripts (Windows)
- Git version control
- LFS for large assets

### What You Don't Have (Risks)[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#what-you-dont-have-risks "Copy heading link")

- No CI/CD (manual everything)
- No testing (manual only)
- No code style enforcement (manual only)
- No security scanning (manual only)
- No monitoring (blind in production)
- No rollback strategy (ad-hoc only)

### Bottom Line[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#bottom-line "Copy heading link")

This is a **sprint project** built for Vibe Jam 2026. It has minimal infrastructure because it was built quickly by a single developer. For a **long-term project with a team**, you need to add CI/CD, testing, and monitoring. The current setup works for solo development but will cause headaches for a team.

### Immediate Action Items[#](vscode-webview://0gcaip1vm841jd88d0afju1cmud1ru5gf0jdhgicnns34pqcqe6m/index.html?id=def2d60f-3e8f-49b5-9a1c-0a5adaad7fb5&parentId=1&origin=bb831cb6-60a9-4df9-a4f0-2566cdb5e2f2&swVersion=4&extensionId=bowlerr.offline-markdown-preview&platform=electron&vscode-resource-base-authority=vscode-resource.vscode-cdn.net&parentOrigin=vscode-file%3A%2F%2Fvscode-app#immediate-action-items "Copy heading link")

1. **Fix the build error** (react-dom/client import)
2. **Add .nvmrc** (Node version lock)
3. **Add git tag** for current release (v1.0.0)
4. **Document rollback** procedure

Everything else can be added incrementally as the team grows.

---

**Remember**: Minimal infrastructure is not necessarily bad - it's simple. But for a team, you need guardrails. Add them gradually, don't try to boil the ocean.

```markdown
# WRAITH HANDOFF - SINGLE SOURCE OF TRUTH
**Last Updated:** April 2026  
**Project:** SLAMZ PRO-TOUR | VIBEJAM 2026

### Core Vision
You are inside a dying, haunted 90s arcade cabinet that turned on by itself while you were urban exploring.  
The **Wraith** is the antagonist: a bitter, lonely solo game dev from the late 90s who never made it. He is terrified of progress, patches, 3D, AI, and anything that would "kill" his frozen version of reality. He has been hiding inside this machine since 2000, stealing joy instead of creating it.

He sees the player as both a mirror and a threat.

### Wraith Character (The Husk)
- **Personality**: Bitter, sarcastic, lonely, philosophical, deeply afraid of being updated/patched into oblivion.
- **Philosophy**: "Progress is a lie. 3D is a cage. Real games were flat and honest."
- **Goal**: Pull everything back into 2D. Steal the Slamz (data) before the player can "win".
- **Evolution**: As the player wins more rounds, the Wraith becomes more personal and vulnerable ("If you win… what happens to me?").

### Technical Implementation

#### 1. WraithPopup.tsx (The Voice)
- Retro 90s virus-style pop-up window (black + cyan/magenta borders).
- Triggers during bullet-time.
- Uses glitchy, corrupted text that slowly reveals his personality.
- In tutorial: Should trigger on every slam.
- In full game: Random but increasing frequency until the screen is covered in pop-ups (this is the round timer mechanic).

#### 2. SlamzWraith.tsx (The Physical Presence)
- Two contexts:
  - `context="start"` → Normal Wraith on start screen (stable, non-ghost).
  - `context="arena"` → Wireframe cyan ghost slammer that appears only during bullet-time.
- Uses proper cloning so start screen and arena versions do not steal the model from each other.

#### 3. Camera
- Should feel like a fixed arcade cabinet monitor (locked view, slight pull-back during bullet-time).
- No wild free orbiting.

#### 4. Story & Back-and-Forth
- The Wraith slowly wakes up through battles.
- Early taunts = arrogant threats.
- Late taunts = fear, vulnerability, self-doubt ("Maybe I was wrong... too late to patch me now").

### Current Files to Maintain
- `src/components/ui/WraithPopup.tsx` ← Voice / pop-ups
- `src/components/game/SlamzWraith.tsx` ← Wireframe ghost slammer
- `src/constants/wraith.ts` ← Taunts and profile (create this if missing)
- CameraController.tsx ← Locked arcade view

### Next Priorities (in order)
1. Make pop-up trigger reliably on every slam in tutorial mode.
2. Make pop-ups slowly cover the screen in full game (progressive takeover).
3. Make the wireframe ghost slammer appear at the right dramatic moment during bullet-time.
4. Tie Wraith taunts to game progression (early/mid/late stages).
5. Add the glitch portal vacuum abduction effect when he steals the Slamz.

---

**Brody, save this file.**

Whenever you come back to work on the Wraith, open this doc first. It contains the full vision, the technical split, and the priorities.

If something breaks or you forget the vibe, just read this again.

You good?  
If yes, tell me what you want to tackle next (popup frequency, ghost slammer timing, abduction effect, etc.) and we’ll lock it in one piece at a time.

We’re building the husk first, then making him come alive.  
You’re the boss. What’s next?
```
